<Pictures>None< /Pictures><Name>LeRoy Lopez</Name>< text>
I have been a loyal customer to Firestone for over 5 years now. Sadly this is my first and possibly my last horrible experience with this company if this does not get resolved in a timely matter.

I took the vehicle in for full synthetic oil change and as soon as I left the store, the check engine light came on. I called the store and told them what happened so they said I could bring it back in to get it looked at.

When I finally brought the vehicle back in to the shop I let Johnny know about the issues. Ie. The check engine light came on as soon ad I left and the vehicle started shifting abnormally hard. (The hard shifting is more than likely unrelated to the oil change, but I expected the car to get an inspection).

I left the car with Firestone for a few hours and upon my return I was greeted with, "there nothing was wrong, there must have been air in the line. The code is cleared and your vehicle is as good as new." Which was my first red flag.

As I leave Firestone and turn onto Zinfandel the check engine light came back on. Which tells me a few things. 1. They did a bold face lie to thier customer about the services being preformed.  2. The only service preformed was clearing the code.  3. Another bold face lie about not being able to inspect the transmission or it's fluids because there is no "dipstick."

Now, I am not a professional mechanic, but I do have project cars and I do take care of the vehicles on my own when I have time for it. But there is other reasons that a transmission will slip and there is other parts of the vehicle that need inspecting if the vehicle is shifting hard. He could have checked the fluid levels by taking the plug out on the side of the transmission. The Chevy Cavalier has a transmission plug on the side very similar to that of a manual transmission. He could have inspected the filter for clogs or leaks. They could have inspected the transmission and/or axels for leaks or cracks. I'm sure they could have checked hoses and the pump. Point is, numerous things could have been checked and they we're not because there is no dipstick.

If you are the manager or owner of this store you can expect a phone call from me tomorrow morning.<//text>

< Review>
The food itself is five stars; the service however leaves so much to be desired. First issues came about when the server asked whether we wanted our soup to be 'lemongrass' or coconut milk--as far as we were aware, the broth would contain lemongrass with or without the addition of coconut milk. This made ordering confusing.
The same server forgot to add one of the dishes to the meal, and came back later saying she didn't put it in, after we had received our previous dishes.
But the real kicker was how the server kept neglecting our table, whenever I needed a water refill, I had to ask some other available server. Our server kept going to the other half of the restaurant where I witnessed her and other servers doing their hair! It would have been hilarious if it didn't mess up our dining experience. I don't even know if she washed her hands after touching her co-worker's hair.
At the end of the meal, the server brought out a scoop of ice cream 'on the house'. In my opinion, it didn't make up for the poor quality service from this young lady.
We've been coming to this restaurant for YEARS, this is the first time we received such terrible service. Will think twice before coming back here again.</Review>
